    3374             : /*
    3375             :  * vcpu_vmx_compute_ctrl
    3376             :  *
    3377             :  * Computes the appropriate control value, given the supplied parameters
    3378             :  * and CPU capabilities.
    3379             :  *
    3380             :  * Intel has made somewhat of a mess of this computation - it is described
    3381             :  * using no fewer than three different approaches, spread across many
    3382             :  * pages of the SDM. Further compounding the problem is the fact that now
    3383             :  * we have "true controls" for each type of "control", and each needs to
    3384             :  * be examined to get the calculation right, but only if "true" controls
    3385             :  * are present on the CPU we're on.
    3386             :  *
    3387             :  * Parameters:
    3388             :  *  ctrlval: the control value, as read from the CPU MSR
    3389             :  *  ctrl: which control is being set (eg, pinbased, procbased, etc)
    3390             :  *  want0: the set of desired 0 bits
    3391             :  *  want1: the set of desired 1 bits
    3392             :  *  out: (out) the correct value to write into the VMCS for this VCPU,
    3393             :  *      for the 'ctrl' desired.
    3394             :  *
    3395             :  * Returns 0 if successful, or EINVAL if the supplied parameters define
    3396             :  *     an unworkable control setup.
    3397             :  */
    3398             : int

    3404             :         /*
    3405             :          * The Intel SDM gives three formulae for determining which bits to
    3406             :          * set/clear for a given control and desired functionality. Formula
    3407             :          * 1 is the simplest but disallows use of newer features that are
    3408             :          * enabled by functionality in later CPUs.
    3409             :          *
    3410             :          * Formulas 2 and 3 allow such extra functionality. We use formula
    3411             :          * 2 - this requires us to know the identity of controls in the
    3412             :          * "default1" class for each control register, but allows us to not
    3413             :          * have to pass along and/or query both sets of capability MSRs for
    3414             :          * each control lookup. This makes the code slightly longer,
    3415             :          * however.
    3416             :          */

    3420           0 :                 clear = ((1ULL << i) & ((uint64_t)ctrlval)) == 0;
